[gymnosperm_genus.n.01] gymnosperm genus -- a genus of gymnosperms
[gymnosperm.n.01] gymnosperm -- plants of the class Gymnospermae having seeds not enclosed in an ovary
[gymnospermous_tree.n.01] gymnospermous tree -- any tree of the division Gymnospermophyta
[gymnospermous_yellowwood.n.01] gymnospermous yellowwood -- any of various gymnospermous trees having yellow wood
[gymnosporangium.n.01] Gymnosporangium -- genus of fungi that produce galls on cedars and other conifers of genera Juniperus and Libocedrus and causes rust spots on apples and pears and other plants of family Rosaceae
[gymnura.n.01] Gymnura -- butterfly rays
[gym_rat.n.01] gym rat -- someone who spends all leisure time playing sports or working out in a gymnasium or health spa
[gym_shoe.n.01] gym shoe -- a canvas shoe with a pliable rubber sole
[gymslip.n.01] gymslip -- a sleeveless tunic worn by English girls as part of a school uniform
[gym_suit.n.01] gym suit -- clothes prescribed for wear while participating in gymnastic exercise
[gynecocracy.n.01] gynecocracy -- a political system governed by a woman
[gynecologist.n.01] gynecologist -- a specialist in gynecology
[gynecology.n.01] gynecology -- the branch of medicine that deals with the diseases and hygiene of women
[gynecomastia.n.01] gynecomastia -- excessive development of the breasts in males; usually the result of hormonal imbalance or treatment with certain drugs (including some antihypertensives)
[gyneolatry.n.01] gyneolatry -- the worship of women
[gynobase.n.01] gynobase -- the enlarged receptacle in which the pistil is borne
[gynoecium.n.01] gynoecium -- a female gametoecium
[gynogenesis.n.01] gynogenesis -- female parthenogenesis in which the embryo contains only maternal chromosomes due to the failure of the sperm to fuse with the egg nucleus
[gynophobia.n.01] gynophobia -- a morbid fear of women
[gynophore.n.01] gynophore -- the stalk of a pistil that raises it above the receptacle
[gynostegium.n.01] gynostegium -- the crown of the stamen in plants of the genus Asclepias
[gynura.n.01] Gynura -- genus of Old World tropical herbs: velvet plants
[gypaetus.n.01] Gypaetus -- in some classifications the type genus of the family Aegypiidae
[gyps.n.01] Gyps -- a genus of Accipitridae
[gypsophila.n.01] Gypsophila -- Mediterranean herbs having small white or pink flowers
[gypsum.n.01] gypsum -- a common white or colorless mineral (hydrated calcium sulphate) used to make cements and plasters (especially plaster of Paris) Also a hyponym of: calcium_sulphate.n.01.
[gypsy_cab.n.01] gypsy cab -- a taxicab that cruises for customers although it is licensed only to respond to calls
[gypsy_moth.n.01] gypsy moth -- European moth introduced into North America; a serious pest of shade trees
[gypsy.n.02] Gypsy -- a member of a people with dark skin and hair who speak Romany and who traditionally live by seasonal work and fortunetelling; they are believed to have originated in northern India but now are living on all continents (but mostly in Europe, North Africa, and North America)
[gyration.n.02] gyration -- the act of rotating in a circle or spiral
[gyrfalcon.n.01] gyrfalcon -- large and rare Arctic falcon having white and dark color phases
[gyrinidae.n.01] Gyrinidae -- whirligig beetles
[gyrocompass.n.01] gyrocompass -- a compass that does not depend on magnetism but uses a gyroscope instead
[gyromitra_californica.n.01] Gyromitra californica -- a gyromitra with a brown puffed up fertile part and a thick fluted stalk; found under conifers in California
[gyromitra_esculenta.n.01] Gyromitra esculenta -- a poisonous gyromitra; the surface of the fertile body is smooth at first and becomes progressively undulating and wrinkled (but never truly pitted); color varies from dull yellow to brown
[gyromitra_fastigiata.n.01] Gyromitra fastigiata -- a lorchel with deep brownish red fertile part and white stalk
[gyromitra_gigas.n.01] Gyromitra gigas -- a gyromitra with a large irregular stalk and fertile part that is yellow to brown and wrinkled; has early fruiting time
[gyromitra_infula.n.01] Gyromitra infula -- a poisonous fungus; saddle-shaped and dull yellow to brown fertile part is relatively even
[gyromitra.n.01] gyromitra -- any fungus of the genus Gyromitra
[gyromitra_sphaerospora.n.01] Gyromitra sphaerospora -- a gyromitra with a brown puffed up fertile part and a rosy pink fluted stalk and smooth round spores; found on hardwood slash east of the Great Plains
[gyro.n.01] gyro -- a Greek sandwich: sliced roast lamb with onion and tomato stuffed into pita bread
[gyroscope.n.01] gyroscope -- rotating mechanism in the form of a universally mounted spinning wheel that offers resistance to turns in any direction
[gyrostabilizer.n.01] gyrostabilizer -- a stabilizer consisting of a heavy gyroscope that spins on a vertical axis; reduces side-to-side rolling of a ship or plane
[gyrus.n.01] gyrus -- a convex fold or elevation in the surface of the brain
